# Ontocode Internal Crate Rename Tracking

Source plan: `ONTOCODE_INTERNAL_CRATE_RENAME_PROJECT_PLAN.md`

## Status Key

- `pending`: not started.
- `in_progress`: assigned or being worked.
- `review`: worker completed; manager review pending.
- `blocked`: cannot proceed safely.
- `done`: accepted and verified.
